===== F:\legendarytopup\app\admin\login\page.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { createClient } from "../../lib/supabase/client";

export default function AdminLoginPage() {
  const router = useRouter();
  const supabase = createClient();

  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  async function handleLogin() {
    if (!email.trim() || !password.trim()) return;
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);

    const { data, error } = await supabase.auth.signInWithPassword({
      email,
      password,
    });

    if (error || !data.user) {
      setLoading(false);
      setError("РќРµРІРµСЂРЅС‹Р№ email РёР»Рё РїР°СЂРѕР»СЊ");
      return;
    }

    // РљР»РёРµРЅС‚СЃРєР°СЏ РїСЂРѕРІРµСЂРєР° РґР»СЏ Р±С‹СЃС‚СЂРѕРіРѕ С„РёРґР±РµРєР°.
    // РќР°СЃС‚РѕСЏС‰Р°СЏ Р·Р°С‰РёС‚Р° вЂ” РІ middleware.ts РЅР° СЃРµСЂРІРµСЂРµ.
    const adminEmail = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_ADMIN_EMAIL;
    if (adminEmail && data.user.email !== adminEmail) {
      await supabase.auth.signOut();
      setLoading(false);
      setError("Р­С‚РѕС‚ Р°РєРєР°СѓРЅС‚ РЅРµ РёРјРµРµС‚ РґРѕСЃС‚СѓРїР° Рє Р°РґРјРёРЅРєРµ");
      return;
    }

    router.push("/admin/support");
    router.refresh();
  }

  return (
    <main className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 px-4 text-white">
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/80 p-6 backdrop-blur">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">Р’С…РѕРґ РІ Р°РґРјРёРЅРєСѓ</h1>

        <div className="mt-6 space-y-4">
          <div>
            <label className="mb-2 block text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-300">
              Email
            </label>
            <input
              type="email"
              value={email}
              onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleLogin()}
              className="w-full rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950 p-3 outline-none transition-colors duration-200 focus:border-violet-500"
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="mb-2 block text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-300">
              РџР°СЂРѕР»СЊ
            </label>
            <input
              type="password"
              value={password}
              onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleLogin()}
              className="w-full rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950 p-3 outline-none transition-colors duration-200 focus:border-violet-500"
            />
          </div>

          {error && <p className="text-sm text-red-400">{error}</p>}

          <button
            onClick={handleLogin}
            disabled={loading}
            className="w-full rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-r from-violet-600 to-violet-500 py-3 font-bold transition-all duration-200 hover:shadow-lg hover:shadow-violet-900/40 active:scale-[0.98] disabled:opacity-50"
          >
            {loading ? "Р’С…РѕРґ..." : "Р’РѕР№С‚Рё"}
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}


===== F:\legendarytopup\app\admin\support\page.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from "react";
import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
import { createClient } from "../../lib/supabase/client";

type Message = {
  id: string;
  session_id: string;
  sender: string;
  message: string;
  created_at: string;
};

const QUICK_REPLIES = [
  "Р—РґСЂР°РІСЃС‚РІСѓР№С‚Рµ! Р§РµРј РјРѕР¶РµРј РїРѕРјРѕС‡СЊ?",
  "РћРїР»Р°С‚Р° РїРѕРґС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґРµРЅР° вњ… РўРѕРІР°СЂ Р·Р°С‡РёСЃР»РµРЅ РЅР° Р°РєРєР°СѓРЅС‚.",
  "РџСЂРѕРІРµСЂСЏРµРј РІР°С€ РїР»Р°С‚С‘Р¶, РїРѕРґРѕР¶РґРёС‚Рµ РїР°СЂСѓ РјРёРЅСѓС‚.",
  "РџСЂРёС€Р»РёС‚Рµ, РїРѕР¶Р°Р»СѓР№СЃС‚Р°, СЃРєСЂРёРЅС€РѕС‚ С‡РµРєР°.",
  "РЎРїР°СЃРёР±Рѕ Р·Р° РѕР±СЂР°С‰РµРЅРёРµ! Р•СЃР»Рё РїРѕСЏРІСЏС‚СЃСЏ РІРѕРїСЂРѕСЃС‹ вЂ” РїРёС€РёС‚Рµ.",
];

function formatTime(iso: string) {
  const date = new Date(iso);
  return date.toLocaleTimeString("ru-RU", {
    hour: "2-digit",
    minute: "2-digit",
  });
}

export default function AdminSupportPage() {
  const supabase = createClient();
  const router = useRouter();
  const [checkingAuth, setCheckingAuth] = useState(true);
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([]);
  const [sessionStatus, setSessionStatus] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
  const [activeSession, setActiveSession] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [reply, setReply] = useState("");
  const [seenSessions, setSeenSessions] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
  const [search, setSearch] = useState("");
  const [userTyping, setUserTyping] = useState(false);
  const [showArchived, setShowArchived] = useState(false);
  const [showQuickReplies, setShowQuickReplies] = useState(false);

  const roomChannelRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof supabase.channel> | null>(null);
  const typingTimeoutRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
  const activeSessionRef = useRef<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    activeSessionRef.current = activeSession;
  }, [activeSession]);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function checkAuth() {
      const { data } = await supabase.auth.getSession();
      if (!data.session) {
        router.push("/admin/login");
        return;
      }
      setCheckingAuth(false);
    }
    checkAuth();

    const { data: listener } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange((_event, session) => {
      if (!session) {
        router.push("/admin/login");
      }
    });

    return () => {
      listener.subscription.unsubscribe();
    };
  }, [router]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (checkingAuth) return;

    const presenceChannel = supabase.channel("admin_presence");
    presenceChannel.subscribe(async (status) => {
      if (status === "SUBSCRIBED") {
        await presenceChannel.track({ online_at: new Date().toISOString() });
      }
    });

    return () => {
      supabase.removeChannel(presenceChannel);
    };
  }, [checkingAuth]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (checkingAuth) return;
    loadMessages();
    loadSessionStatuses();
  }, [checkingAuth]);

  async function loadMessages() {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from("support_messages")
      .select("*")
      .order("created_at", { ascending: true });
    if (data) setMessages(data as Message[]);
  }

  async function loadSessionStatuses() {
    const { data } = await supabase.from("support_sessions").select("*");
    if (data) {
      const map: Record<string, string> = {};
      data.forEach((row: { session_id: string; status: string }) => {
        map[row.session_id] = row.status;
      });
      setSessionStatus(map);
    }
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    if (checkingAuth) return;

    const channel = supabase
      .channel("support_room", {
        config: { broadcast: { self: false } },
      })
      .on("broadcast", { event: "message" }, ({ payload }) => {
        const incoming = payload as Message;

        setMessages((prev) =>
          prev.some((m) => m.id === incoming.id) ? prev : [...prev, incoming]
        );

        if (incoming.sender === "user") {
          if (incoming.session_id !== activeSessionRef.current) {
            setSeenSessions((prev) => {
              const next = new Set(prev);
              next.delete(incoming.session_id);
              return next;
            });
          }
          try {
            new Audio(
              "data:audio/wav;base64,UklGRhwAAABXQVZFZm10IBAAAAABAAEAQB8AAEAfAAABAAgAZGF0YQAAAAA="
            ).play();
          } catch {}
        }
      })
      .on("broadcast", { event: "typing" }, ({ payload }) => {
        if (payload.sender !== "user") return;
        if (payload.session_id !== activeSessionRef.current) return;
        setUserTyping(true);
        if (typingTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(typingTimeoutRef.current);
        typingTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => setUserTyping(false), 2500);
      })
      .on("broadcast", { event: "session_status" }, ({ payload }) => {
        setSessionStatus((prev) => ({
          ...prev,
          [payload.session_id]: payload.status,
        }));
      })
      .subscribe();

    roomChannelRef.current = channel;

    return () => {
      supabase.removeChannel(channel);
    };
  }, [checkingAuth]);

  useEffect(() => {
    setUserTyping(false);
    setShowQuickReplies(false);
  }, [activeSession]);

  async function handleLogout() {
    await supabase.auth.signOut();
    router.push("/admin/login");
  }

  const allSessions = Array.from(new Set(messages.map((m) => m.session_id))).sort(
    (a, b) => {
      const lastA = messages.filter((m) => m.session_id === a).slice(-1)[0];
      const lastB = messages.filter((m) => m.session_id === b).slice(-1)[0];
      return (
        new Date(lastB?.created_at ?? 0).getTime() -
        new Date(lastA?.created_at ?? 0).getTime()
      );
    }
  );

  function lastMessage(sessionId: string) {
    const msgs = messages.filter((m) => m.session_id === sessionId);
    return msgs[msgs.length - 1];
  }

  function isClosed(sessionId: string) {
    return sessionStatus[sessionId] === "closed";
  }

  function hasUnread(sessionId: string) {
    const last = lastMessage(sessionId);
    return (
      last?.sender === "user" &&
      sessionId !== activeSession &&
      !seenSessions.has(sessionId) &&
      !isClosed(sessionId)
    );
  }

  const visibleSessions = allSessions.filter((s) =>
    showArchived ? isClosed(s) : !isClosed(s)
  );

  const sessions = visibleSessions.filter((sessionId) => {
    if (!search.trim()) return true;
    const last = lastMessage(sessionId);
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return (
      sessionId.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      last?.message?.toLowerCase().includes(q)
    );
  });

  const totalUnread = allSessions.filter((s) => hasUnread(s)).length;

  const activeMessages = messages.filter((m) => m.session_id === activeSession);

  function openSession(sessionId: string) {
    setActiveSession(sessionId);
    setSeenSessions((prev) => new Set(prev).add(sessionId));
  }

  async function toggleArchive(sessionId: string) {
    const newStatus = isClosed(sessionId) ? "open" : "closed";
    setSessionStatus((prev) => ({ ...prev, [sessionId]: newStatus }));

    await supabase
      .from("support_sessions")
      .upsert({ session_id: sessionId, status: newStatus, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() });

    roomChannelRef.current?.send({
      type: "broadcast",
      event: "session_status",
      payload: { session_id: sessionId, status: newStatus },
    });

    if (newStatus === "closed") setActiveSession(null);
  }

  function handleReplyChange(value: string) {
    setReply(value);
    if (!activeSession) return;
    roomChannelRef.current?.send({
      type: "broadcast",
      event: "typing",
      payload: { sender: "admin", session_id: activeSession },
    });
  }

  function insertQuickReply(templateText: string) {
    setReply(templateText);
    setShowQuickReplies(false);
  }

  async function handleReply() {
    const trimmed = reply.trim();
    if (!trimmed || !activeSession) return;

    const tempId = `temp-${Date.now()}`;
    const optimisticMessage: Message = {
      id: tempId,
      session_id: activeSession,
      sender: "admin",
      message: trimmed,
      created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    setMessages((prev) => [...prev, optimisticMessage]);
    setReply("");

    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from("support_messages")
      .insert({ session_id: activeSession, sender: "admin", message: trimmed })
      .select()
      .single();

    if (error) {
      setMessages((prev) => prev.filter((m) => m.id !== tempId));
      return;
    }

    const saved = data as Message;
    setMessages((prev) => prev.map((m) => (m.id === tempId ? saved : m)));

    roomChannelRef.current?.send({
      type: "broadcast",
      event: "message",
      payload: saved,
    });
  }

  if (checkingAuth) {
    return (
      <main className="flex h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 text-white">
        <span className="h-10 w-10 animate-spin rounded-full border-4 border-zinc-700 border-t-violet-500" />
      </main>
    );
  }

  return (
    <main className="flex h-screen bg-zinc-950 text-white">
      <div
        className={`flex w-full shrink-0 flex-col border-r border-zinc-800 md:block md:w-80 ${
          activeSession ? "hidden md:flex" : "flex"
        }`}
      >
        <div className="border-b border-zinc-800 p-4">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <h1 className="text-lg font-bold">РћР±СЂР°С‰РµРЅРёСЏ</h1>
              <div className="mt-1 flex items-center gap-3 text-xs text-zinc-500">
                <span>{sessions.length} РґРёР°Р»РѕРіРѕРІ</span>
                {totalUnread > 0 && !showArchived && (
                  <span className="flex items-center gap-1 font-semibold text-violet-400">
                    <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full bg-violet-500" />
                    {totalUnread} РЅРѕРІС‹С…
                  </span>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={handleLogout}
              className="text-xs text-zinc-500 transition-colors duration-150 hover:text-white"
            >
              Р’С‹Р№С‚Рё
            </button>
          </div>

          <input
            value={search}
            onChange={(e) => setSearch(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="РџРѕРёСЃРє РїРѕ РґРёР°Р»РѕРіР°Рј..."
            className="mt-3 w-full rounded-lg border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm outline-none transition-colors duration-200 focus:border-violet-500"
          />

          <div className="mt-3 flex gap-1 rounded-lg bg-zinc-900 p-1 text-xs">
            <button
              onClick={() => setShowArchived(false)}
              className={`flex-1 rounded-md py-1.5 font-semibold transition-colors duration-150 ${
                !showArchived ? "bg-violet-600 text-white" : "text-zinc-500 hover:text-zinc-300"
              }`}
            >
              РђРєС‚РёРІРЅС‹Рµ
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={() => setShowArchived(true)}
              className={`flex-1 rounded-md py-1.5 font-semibold transition-colors duration-150 ${
                showArchived ? "bg-violet-600 text-white" : "text-zinc-500 hover:text-zinc-300"
              }`}
            >
              РђСЂС…РёРІ
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto">
          {sessions.map((sessionId) => {
            const last = lastMessage(sessionId);
            const unread = hasUnread(sessionId);
            return (
              <button
                key={sessionId}
                onClick={() => openSession(sessionId)}
                className={`flex w-full items-start justify-between gap-2 border-b border-zinc-900 p-4 text-left transition-colors duration-150 hover:bg-zinc-900 ${
                  activeSession === sessionId ? "bg-zinc-900" : ""
                }`}
              >
                <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <p className="text-xs text-zinc-500">
                      {sessionId.slice(0, 8)}...
                    </p>
                    {last && (
                      <p className="text-xs text-zinc-600">
                        {formatTime(last.created_at)}
                      </p>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <p
                    className={`mt-1 truncate text-sm ${
                      unread ? "font-semibold text-white" : "text-zinc-300"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {last?.sender === "admin" ? "Р’С‹: " : ""}
                    {last?.message}
                  </p>
                </div>
                {unread && (
                  <span className="mt-1 h-2 w-2 shrink-0 animate-pulse rounded-full bg-violet-500" />
                )}
              </button>
            );
          })}

          {sessions.length === 0 && (
            <p className="p-4 text-sm text-zinc-500">
              {search
                ? "РќРёС‡РµРіРѕ РЅРµ РЅР°Р№РґРµРЅРѕ"
                : showArchived
                ? "РђСЂС…РёРІ РїСѓСЃС‚"
                : "РџРѕРєР° РЅРµС‚ РѕР±СЂР°С‰РµРЅРёР№"}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className={`flex-1 flex-col ${activeSession ? "flex" : "hidden md:flex"}`}>
        {!activeSession ? (
          <div className="flex flex-1 items-center justify-center text-zinc-500">
            Р’С‹Р±РµСЂРёС‚Рµ РґРёР°Р»РѕРі СЃР»РµРІР°
          </div>
        ) : (
          <>
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3 border-b border-zinc-800 p-4">
              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <button
                  onClick={() => setActiveSession(null)}
                  className="text-zinc-400 transition-colors duration-150 hover:text-white md:hidden"
                >
                  в†ђ РќР°Р·Р°Рґ
                </button>
                <p className="text-sm text-zinc-500">{activeSession.slice(0, 8)}...</p>
              </div>

              <button
                onClick={() => toggleArchive(activeSession)}
                className="rounded-lg border border-zinc-700 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-zinc-300 transition-colors duration-150 hover:bg-zinc-800"
              >
                {isClosed(activeSession) ? "в†© Р’РµСЂРЅСѓС‚СЊ РІ Р°РєС‚РёРІРЅС‹Рµ" : "вњ“ Р—Р°РєСЂС‹С‚СЊ РґРёР°Р»РѕРі"}
              </button>
            </div>

            <div className="flex-1 space-y-3 overflow-y-auto p-4 sm:p-6">
              {activeMessages.map((m) => (
                <div
                  key={m.id}
                  className={`flex flex-col ${
                    m.sender === "admin" ? "items-end" : "items-start"
                  }`}
                >
                  <div
                    className={`animate-fade-in max-w-[85%] rounded-xl px-4 py-2 text-sm sm:max-w-md ${
                      m.sender === "admin"
                        ? "bg-violet-600 text-white"
                        : "bg-zinc-800 text-white"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {m.message}
                  </div>
                  <span className="mt-1 px-1 text-[10px] text-zinc-500">
                    {formatTime(m.created_at)}
                  </span>
                </div>
              ))}

              {userTyping && (
                <div className="animate-fade-in flex items-center gap-1 px-1">
                  <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-bounce rounded-full bg-zinc-500 [animation-delay:-0.3s]" />
                  <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-bounce rounded-full bg-zinc-500 [animation-delay:-0.15s]" />
                  <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-bounce rounded-full bg-zinc-500" />
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

            {showQuickReplies && (
              <div className="animate-fade-in flex flex-wrap gap-2 border-t border-zinc-800 p-3">
                {QUICK_REPLIES.map((qr) => (
                  <button
                    key={qr}
                    onClick={() => insertQuickReply(qr)}
                    className="rounded-full border border-zinc-700 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs text-zinc-300 transition-colors duration-150 hover:border-violet-500 hover:bg-violet-500/10 hover:text-white"
                  >
                    {qr.length > 40 ? qr.slice(0, 40) + "вЂ¦" : qr}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="flex gap-2 border-t border-zinc-800 p-3 sm:p-4">
              <button
                onClick={() => setShowQuickReplies((v) => !v)}
                title="Р‘С‹СЃС‚СЂС‹Рµ РѕС‚РІРµС‚С‹"
                className={`shrink-0 rounded-lg border px-3 text-sm transition-colors duration-150 ${
                  showQuickReplies
                    ? "border-violet-500 bg-violet-500/10 text-violet-400"
                    : "border-zinc-700 text-zinc-400 hover:bg-zinc-800"
                }`}
              >
                вљЎ
              </button>
              <input
                value={reply}
                onChange={(e) => handleReplyChange(e.target.value)}
                onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === "Enter" && handleReply()}
                placeholder="Р’Р°С€ РѕС‚РІРµС‚..."
                className="flex-1 rounded-lg border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-900 px-3 py-2 text-sm outline-none transition-colors duration-200 focus:border-violet-500"
              />
              <button
                onClick={handleReply}
                className="rounded-lg bg-violet-600 px-5 py-2 text-sm font-bold transition-all duration-200 hover:bg-violet-500 active:scale-95"
              >
                РћС‚РїСЂР°РІРёС‚СЊ
              </button>
            </div>
          </>
        )}
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}

    { label: "Р—Р°РєР°Р·С‹", href: "/admin" },

      </Link>

          <Link
            key={tab.href}
            href={tab.href}
            className={`rounded-lg border px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-semibold transition ${
              pathname === tab.href
                ? "border-violet-500 bg-violet-600"
                : "border-zinc-700 hover:bg-zinc-900"
            }`}

            {tab.label}

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useAuth } from "../context/AuthContext";
import { supabase } from "../lib/supabaseClient";
import AdminNav from "./AdminNav";

const ADMIN_EMAIL = "sarvarmirzaliyev21@gmail.com";

type Order = {
  id: string;
  created_at: string;
  game: string;
  product: string;
  price_usd: number;
  price_sum: number;
  receipt_url: string | null;
  player_info: string | null;
  status: string;
};

const STATUS_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  РѕР¶РёРґР°РµС‚_РїРѕРґС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґРµРЅРёСЏ: "РћР¶РёРґР°РµС‚ РїРѕРґС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґРµРЅРёСЏ",
  РѕРїР»Р°С‡РµРЅРѕ: "РћРїР»Р°С‡РµРЅРѕ",
  РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРѕ: "Р’С‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРѕ",
  РѕС‚РєР»РѕРЅРµРЅРѕ: "РћС‚РєР»РѕРЅРµРЅРѕ",
};

const STATUS_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  РѕР¶РёРґР°РµС‚_РїРѕРґС‚РІРµСЂР¶РґРµРЅРёСЏ: "bg-yellow-950/50 text-yellow-400 border-yellow-800",
  РѕРїР»Р°С‡РµРЅРѕ: "bg-blue-950/50 text-blue-400 border-blue-800",
  РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРѕ: "bg-emerald-950/50 text-emerald-400 border-emerald-800",
  РѕС‚РєР»РѕРЅРµРЅРѕ: "bg-red-950/50 text-red-400 border-red-800",
};

function formatDate(iso: string) {
  return new Date(iso).toLocaleString("ru-RU", {
    day: "numeric",
    month: "short",
    hour: "2-digit",
    minute: "2-digit",
  });
}

function parsePlayerInfo(raw: string | null) {
  if (!raw) return {};
  try {
    return JSON.parse(raw) as Record<string, string>;
  } catch {
    return {};
  }
}

function PinGate({ onVerified }: { onVerified: () => void }) {
  const [pin, setPin] = useState("");
  const [error, setError] = useState(false);
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);

  async function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    setSubmitting(true);
    setError(false);

    const res = await fetch("/api/admin-pin", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ pin }),
    });

    setSubmitting(false);

    if (res.ok) {
      onVerified();
    } else {
      setError(true);
      setPin("");
    }
  }

  return (
    <main className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 px-4 text-white">
      <form
        onSubmit={handleSubmit}
        className="w-full max-w-sm rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-6"
      >
        <div className="mb-4 text-center text-4xl">рџ”ђ</div>
        <h1 className="text-center text-xl font-bold">РљРѕРґ РґРѕСЃС‚СѓРїР°</h1>
        <p className="mt-1 text-center text-sm text-zinc-400">
          Р’РІРµРґРёС‚Рµ PIN-РєРѕРґ РґР»СЏ РІС…РѕРґР° РІ РїР°РЅРµР»СЊ РІР»Р°РґРµР»СЊС†Р°
        </p>

        <input
          type="password"
          inputMode="numeric"
          autoFocus
          value={pin}
          onChange={(e) => setPin(e.target.value)}
          className="mt-5 w-full rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950 p-3 text-center text-lg tracking-widest outline-none focus:border-violet-500"
          placeholder="вЂўвЂўвЂўвЂў"
        />

        {error && (
          <p className="mt-2 text-center text-sm text-red-400">
            РќРµРІРµСЂРЅС‹Р№ РєРѕРґ, РїРѕРїСЂРѕР±СѓР№С‚Рµ РµС‰С‘ СЂР°Р·
          </p>
        )}

        <button
          type="submit"
          disabled={submitting || pin.length === 0}
          className="mt-4 w-full rounded-xl bg-violet-600 py-3 font-semibold transition hover:bg-violet-500 disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          {submitting ? "РџСЂРѕРІРµСЂРєР°..." : "Р’РѕР№С‚Рё"}
        </button>
      </form>
    </main>
  );
}

export default function AdminPage() {
  const { user, loading: authLoading } = useAuth();

  const [orders, setOrders] = useState<Order[]>([]);
  const [loadingOrders, setLoadingOrders] = useState(true);
  const [updatingId, setUpdatingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<string>("РІСЃРµ");

  const [pinChecked, setPinChecked] = useState(false);
  const [pinVerified, setPinVerified] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetch("/api/admin-pin")
      .then((res) => res.json())
      .then((data) => {
        setPinVerified(!!data.ok);
        setPinChecked(true);
      })
      .catch(() => setPinChecked(true));
  }, []);

  async function loadOrders() {
    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from("orders")
      .select("*")
      .order("created_at", { ascending: false });

    if (!error && data) setOrders(data as Order[]);
    setLoadingOrders(false);
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    if (user?.email === ADMIN_EMAIL && pinVerified) {
      loadOrders();
    } else {
      setLoadingOrders(false);
    }
  }, [user, pinVerified]);

  async function updateStatus(id: string, status: string) {
    setUpdatingId(id);
    const { error } = await supabase
      .from("orders")
      .update({ status })
      .eq("id", id);

    if (!error) {
      setOrders((prev) =>
        prev.map((o) => (o.id === id ? { ...o, status } : o))
      );
    }
    setUpdatingId(null);
  }

  if (authLoading || !pinChecked) {
    return (
      <main className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 text-white">
        Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєР°...
      </main>
    );
  }

  if (!user || user.email !== ADMIN_EMAIL) {
    return (
      <main className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 px-4 text-white">
        <div className="text-center">
          <div className="mb-4 text-5xl">рџ”’</div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">Р”РѕСЃС‚СѓРї Р·Р°РїСЂРµС‰С‘РЅ</h1>
          <p className="mt-2 text-zinc-400">
            Р­С‚Р° СЃС‚СЂР°РЅРёС†Р° РґРѕСЃС‚СѓРїРЅР° С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РІР»Р°РґРµР»СЊС†Сѓ СЃР°Р№С‚Р°.
          </p>
        </div>
      </main>
    );
  }

  if (!pinVerified) {
    return <PinGate onVerified={() => setPinVerified(true)} />;
  }

  if (loadingOrders) {
    return (
      <main className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 text-white">
        Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєР°...
      </main>
    );
  }

  const filteredOrders =
    filter === "РІСЃРµ" ? orders : orders.filter((o) => o.status === filter);

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-zinc-950 px-4 py-10 text-white sm:px-6 sm:py-16">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-5xl">
        <AdminNav />
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold sm:text-3xl">Р—Р°РєР°Р·С‹</h1>
        <p className="mt-1 text-zinc-400">Р’СЃРµРіРѕ Р·Р°РєР°Р·РѕРІ: {orders.length}</p>

        {/* Р¤РёР»СЊС‚СЂ РїРѕ СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃСѓ */}
        <div className="mt-6 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
          {["РІСЃРµ", ...Object.keys(STATUS_LABELS)].map((s) => (
            <button
              key={s}
              onClick={() => setFilter(s)}
              className={`rounded-lg border px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-semibold transition ${
                filter === s
                  ? "border-violet-500 bg-violet-600"
                  : "border-zinc-700 hover:bg-zinc-900"
              }`}
            >
              {s === "РІСЃРµ" ? "Р’СЃРµ" : STATUS_LABELS[s]}
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* РЎРїРёСЃРѕРє Р·Р°РєР°Р·РѕРІ */}
        <div className="mt-6 space-y-4">
          {filteredOrders.length === 0 && (
            <p className="text-zinc-500">Р—Р°РєР°Р·РѕРІ РЅРµС‚</p>
          )}

          {filteredOrders.map((order) => {
            const playerInfo = parsePlayerInfo(order.player_info);

            return (
              <div
                key={order.id}
                className="rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-5"
              >
                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-3">
                  <div>
                    <p className="text-sm text-zinc-500">
                      {formatDate(order.created_at)}
                    </p>
                    <h3 className="mt-1 text-lg font-bold">
                      {order.game} вЂ” {order.product}
                    </h3>
                    <p className="mt-1 font-bold text-violet-400">
                      ${order.price_usd} В·{" "}
                      {order.price_sum.toLocaleString("ru-RU")} СЃСѓРј
                    </p>
                  </div>

                  <span
                    className={`rounded-lg border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold ${
                      STATUS_COLORS[order.status] ??
                      "border-zinc-700 text-zinc-400"
                    }`}
                  >
                    {STATUS_LABELS[order.status] ?? order.status}
                  </span>
                </div>

                {Object.keys(playerInfo).length > 0 && (
                  <div className="mt-3 space-y-1 border-t border-zinc-800 pt-3">
                    {Object.entries(playerInfo).map(([label, value]) => (
                      <p key={label} className="text-sm text-zinc-400">
                        {label}:{" "}
                        <span className="font-semibold text-white">
                          {value}
                        </span>
                      </p>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}

                {order.receipt_url && (
                  <a
                    href={order.receipt_url}
                    target="_blank"
                    rel="noopener noreferrer"
                    className="mt-3 inline-block text-sm text-violet-400 hover:underline"
                  >
                    рџ“Ћ РџРѕСЃРјРѕС‚СЂРµС‚СЊ С‡РµРє
                  </a>
                )}

                <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2 border-t border-zinc-800 pt-4">
                  <button
                    onClick={() => updateStatus(order.id, "РѕРїР»Р°С‡РµРЅРѕ")}
                    disabled={updatingId === order.id}
                    className="rounded-lg bg-blue-600 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-semibold transition hover:bg-blue-500 disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    РџРѕРґС‚РІРµСЂРґРёС‚СЊ РѕРїР»Р°С‚Сѓ
                  </button>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => updateStatus(order.id, "РІС‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРѕ")}
                    disabled={updatingId === order.id}
                    className="rounded-lg bg-emerald-600 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-semibold transition hover:bg-emerald-500 disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    Р’С‹РїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРѕ
                  </button>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => updateStatus(order.id, "РѕС‚РєР»РѕРЅРµРЅРѕ")}
                    disabled={updatingId === order.id}
                    className="rounded-lg bg-red-600 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-semibold transition hover:bg-red-500 disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    РћС‚РєР»РѕРЅРёС‚СЊ
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </div>

===== F:\legendarytopup\app\api\admin-pin\route.ts =====

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from "next/server";
import { cookies } from "next/headers";
import { COOKIE_NAME, createPinCookieValue, isPinCookieValid } from "../../lib/adminPin";

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const { pin } = await req.json();

  if (!pin || pin !== process.env.ADMIN_PIN) {
    return NextResponse.json({ ok: false }, { status: 401 });
  }

  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  cookieStore.set(COOKIE_NAME, createPinCookieValue(), {
    httpOnly: true,
    secure: true,
    sameSite: "lax",
    path: "/",
    maxAge: 60 * 60 * 12,
  });

  return NextResponse.json({ ok: true });
}

export async function GET() {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();
  const value = cookieStore.get(COOKIE_NAME)?.value;
  return NextResponse.json({ ok: isPinCookieValid(value) });
}

===== F:\legendarytopup\app\components\CheckoutContent.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { useSearchParams } from "next/navigation";
import { paymentDetails } from "../data/payments";
import { EXCHANGE_RATE_UZS_PER_USD } from "../data/games";
import { supabase } from "../lib/supabaseClient";
import { useAuth } from "../context/AuthContext";

export default function CheckoutContent() {
  const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  const { user } = useAuth();

  const game = searchParams.get("game") ?? "РўРѕРІР°СЂ";
  const product = searchParams.get("product") ?? "";
  const price = searchParams.get("price") ?? "";
  const priceUsd = parseFloat(searchParams.get("priceUsd") ?? "0");
  const playerInfoRaw = searchParams.get("playerInfo") ?? "{}";

  let playerInfo: Record<string, string> = {};
  try {
    playerInfo = JSON.parse(playerInfoRaw);
  } catch {
    playerInfo = {};
  }

  const sumAmount = Math.round(priceUsd * EXCHANGE_RATE_UZS_PER_USD);
  const sumAmountFormatted = `${sumAmount.toLocaleString("ru-RU")} СЃСѓРј`;

  const [cardCopied, setCardCopied] = useState(false);
  const [sumCopied, setSumCopied] = useState(false);
  const [receipt, setReceipt] = useState<File | null>(null);
  const [submitted, setSubmitted] = useState(false);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);

  function handleCopyCard() {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(paymentDetails.cardNumber.replace(/\s/g, ""));
    setCardCopied(true);
    setTimeout(() => setCardCopied(false), 2000);
  }

  function handleCopySum() {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(String(sumAmount));
    setSumCopied(true);
    setTimeout(() => setSumCopied(false), 2000);
  }

  async function handleSubmit() {
    if (!receipt) return;

    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);

    try {
      const fileExt = receipt.name.split(".").pop();
      const fileName = `${crypto.randomUUID()}.${fileExt}`;

      const { error: uploadError } = await supabase.storage
        .from("receipts")
        .upload(fileName, receipt);

      if (uploadError) throw uploadError;

      const { data: publicUrlData } = supabase.storage
        .from("receipts")
        .getPublicUrl(fileName);

      const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("orders").insert({
        game,
        product,
        price_usd: priceUsd,
        price_sum: sumAmount,
        receipt_url: publicUrlData.publicUrl,
        player_info: JSON.stringify(playerInfo),
        user_id: user?.id ?? null,
      });

      if (insertError) throw insertError;

      setSubmitted(true);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      setError(
        "РќРµ РїРѕР»СѓС‡РёР»РѕСЃСЊ РѕС‚РїСЂР°РІРёС‚СЊ Р·Р°СЏРІРєСѓ. РџРѕРїСЂРѕР±СѓР№С‚Рµ РµС‰С‘ СЂР°Р· РёР»Рё РЅР°РїРёС€РёС‚Рµ РІ РїРѕРґРґРµСЂР¶РєСѓ."
      );
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }

  if (submitted) {
    return (
      <main className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-zinc-950 px-4 text-white">
        <div className="max-w-md rounded-3xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-8 text-center">
          <div className="mb-4 text-5xl">вњ…</div>
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">Р—Р°СЏРІРєР° РїСЂРёРЅСЏС‚Р°!</h1>
          <p className="mt-3 text-zinc-400">
            РњС‹ РїСЂРѕРІРµСЂРёРј РѕРїР»Р°С‚Сѓ Рё РѕС‚РїСЂР°РІРёРј {product} РЅР° РІР°С€ Р°РєРєР°СѓРЅС‚ РІ С‚РµС‡РµРЅРёРµ
            РЅРµСЃРєРѕР»СЊРєРёС… РјРёРЅСѓС‚. РЎРїР°СЃРёР±Рѕ Р·Р° РїРѕРєСѓРїРєСѓ!
          </p>
        </div>
      </main>
    );
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-zinc-950 px-4 py-10 text-white sm:px-6 sm:py-16">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-xl">
        <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold sm:text-3xl">РћРїР»Р°С‚Р° Р·Р°РєР°Р·Р°</h1>

        {/* РЎРІРѕРґРєР° Р·Р°РєР°Р·Р° */}
        <div className="mt-6 rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-5">
          <p className="text-sm text-zinc-400">{game}</p>
          <p className="mt-1 text-xl font-bold">{product}</p>
          <p className="mt-2 text-2xl font-bold text-violet-400">{price}</p>

          {Object.keys(playerInfo).length > 0 && (
            <div className="mt-4 space-y-1 border-t border-zinc-800 pt-4">
              {Object.entries(playerInfo).map(([label, value]) => (
                <p key={label} className="text-sm text-zinc-400">
                  {label}:{" "}
                  <span className="font-semibold text-white">{value}</span>
                </p>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* РЎСѓРјРјР° Рє РїРµСЂРµРІРѕРґСѓ РІ СЃСѓРјР°С… */}
        <div className="mt-6 rounded-2xl border border-violet-600/50 bg-violet-950/30 p-5">
          <h2 className="text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-400">
            Рљ РїРµСЂРµРІРѕРґСѓ СЂРѕРІРЅРѕ
          </h2>

          <p className="mt-1 text-3xl font-bold tracking-wide">
            {sumAmountFormatted}
          </p>

          <button
            onClick={handleCopySum}
            className="mt-4 w-full rounded-lg border border-violet-600 py-2 text-sm font-semibold transition hover:bg-violet-600/20"
          >
            {sumCopied ? "РЎРєРѕРїРёСЂРѕРІР°РЅРѕ вњ“" : "РЎРєРѕРїРёСЂРѕРІР°С‚СЊ СЃСѓРјРјСѓ"}
          </button>

          <p className="mt-3 text-xs text-zinc-500">
            РџРµСЂРµРІРѕРґРёС‚Рµ СЂРѕРІРЅРѕ СЌС‚Сѓ СЃСѓРјРјСѓ вЂ” С‚Р°Рє РјС‹ Р±С‹СЃС‚СЂРµРµ СЃРІРµСЂРёРј РѕРїР»Р°С‚Сѓ.
          </p>
        </div>

        {/* Р РµРєРІРёР·РёС‚С‹ */}
        <div className="mt-6 rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-5">

          <h2 className="mb-4 text-lg font-bold">РџСЂРёРєСЂРµРїРёС‚Рµ С‡РµРє</h2>

          <label className="flex cursor-pointer flex-col items-center justify-center rounded-xl border-2 border-dashed border-zinc-700 p-8 text-center transition hover:border-violet-500">

              {receipt ? receipt.name : "РќР°Р¶РјРёС‚Рµ, С‡С‚РѕР±С‹ РІС‹Р±СЂР°С‚СЊ СЃРєСЂРёРЅС€РѕС‚"}
            </span>
            <input
              type="file"
              accept="image/*"
              className="hidden"
              onChange={(e) => setReceipt(e.target.files?.[0] ?? null)}
            />
          </label>
        </div>

        {error && (
          <p className="mt-4 rounded-lg bg-red-950/50 p-3 text-center text-sm text-red-400">
            {error}
          </p>
        )}

        <button
          onClick={handleSubmit}
          disabled={!receipt || loading}
          className="mt-6 w-full rounded-2xl bg-violet-600 py-4 text-lg font-bold transition hover:bg-violet-500 disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:bg-zinc-700 disabled:text-zinc-500"
        >
          {loading ? "РћС‚РїСЂР°РІРєР°..." : "РЇ РѕРїР»Р°С‚РёР»"}
        </button>

          <p className="mt-2 text-center text-sm text-zinc-500">
            РЎРЅР°С‡Р°Р»Р° РїСЂРёРєСЂРµРїРёС‚Рµ С‡РµРє, С‡С‚РѕР±С‹ РѕС‚РїСЂР°РІРёС‚СЊ Р·Р°СЏРІРєСѓ
          </p>
        )}
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}

===== F:\legendarytopup\app\components\Navbar.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { useAuth } from "../context/AuthContext";

export default function Navbar() {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const { user, signOut, loading } = useAuth();

  const links = [
    { label: "Игры", href: "#games" },
    { label: "Отзывы", href: "#reviews" },
  ];

  return (
    <header className="sticky top-0 z-50 border-b border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-950/80 backdrop-blur">
      <div className="mx-auto flex max-w-7xl items-center justify-between p-4 sm:p-6">
        <Link href="/" className="text-xl font-bold text-violet-500 sm:text-2xl md:text-3xl">
          LegendaryTopUp
        </Link>

        {/* Меню для десктопа */}
        <nav className="hidden md:flex gap-8 text-white">
          {links.map((link) => (
            <a
              key={link.label}
              href={link.href}
              className="transition hover:text-violet-400"
            >
              {link.label}
            </a>
          ))}
          {!loading && user && (
            <Link
              href="/orders"
              className="transition hover:text-violet-400"
            >
              Мои заказы
            </Link>
          )}
        </nav>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          {!loading && user ? (
            <div className="hidden items-center gap-3 sm:flex">
              <button
                onClick={signOut}
                className="rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold transition hover:bg-zinc-900"
              >
                Выйти
              </button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <Link
              href="/login"
              className="rounded-xl bg-violet-600 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold transition hover:bg-violet-500 sm:px-5 sm:py-2 sm:text-base"
            >
              Войти
            </Link>
          )}

          {/* Кнопка-бургер, видна только на мобильном */}
          <button
            onClick={() => setOpen(!open)}
            aria-label="Открыть меню"
            className="flex h-10 w-10 flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1.5 rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 md:hidden"
          >
            <span
              className={`h-0.5 w-5 bg-white transition ${
                open ? "translate-y-2 rotate-45" : ""
              }`}
            />
            <span
              className={`h-0.5 w-5 bg-white transition ${
                open ? "opacity-0" : ""
              }`}
            />
            <span
              className={`h-0.5 w-5 bg-white transition ${
                open ? "-translate-y-2 -rotate-45" : ""
              }`}
            />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Выпадающее мобильное меню */}
      {open && (
        <nav className="flex flex-col gap-1 border-t border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-950 px-6 py-4 md:hidden">
          {links.map((link) => (
            <a
              key={link.label}
              href={link.href}
              onClick={() => setOpen(false)}
              className="rounded-lg px-3 py-3 text-white transition hover:bg-zinc-900 hover:text-violet-400"
            >
              {link.label}
            </a>
          ))}

          {!loading && user && (
            <Link
              href="/orders"
              onClick={() => setOpen(false)}
              className="rounded-lg px-3 py-3 text-white transition hover:bg-zinc-900 hover:text-violet-400"
            >
              Мои заказы
            </Link>
          )}

          {!loading && user && (
            <button
              onClick={() => {
                signOut();
                setOpen(false);
              }}
              className="rounded-lg px-3 py-3 text-left text-red-400 transition hover:bg-zinc-900"
            >
              Выйти
            </button>
          )}
        </nav>
      )}
    </header>
  );
}

===== F:\legendarytopup\app\components\PurchaseSection.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";

type Field = {
  label: string;
  placeholder: string;
};

type Product = {
  name: string;
  price: number;
  priceDisplay: string;
};

type PurchaseSectionProps = {
  gameName: string;
  fields: Field[];
  products: Product[];
};

export default function PurchaseSection({
  gameName,
  fields,
  products,
}: PurchaseSectionProps) {
  const [fieldValues, setFieldValues] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<string | null>(null);

  function handleFieldChange(label: string, value: string) {
    setFieldValues((prev) => ({ ...prev, [label]: value }));
  }

  function buildPlayerInfo() {
    return fields
      .map((f) => `${f.label}: ${fieldValues[f.label] ?? ""}`)
      .join(", ");
  }

  return (
    <>
      <div className="mt-8 space-y-5 sm:mt-10">
        {fields.map((field) => (
          <div key={field.label}>
            <label className="mb-2 block text-sm font-semibold text-zinc-300">
              {field.label}
            </label>

            <input
              placeholder={field.placeholder}
              value={fieldValues[field.label] ?? ""}
              onChange={(e) => handleFieldChange(field.label, e.target.value)}
              className="w-full rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-900/60 p-4 outline-none backdrop-blur transition-all duration-200 focus:border-violet-500 focus:bg-zinc-900 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-violet-500/20"
            />
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      <div className="mt-8 sm:mt-10">
        <h2 className="mb-5 text-xl font-bold sm:text-2xl">
          Р’С‹Р±РµСЂРёС‚Рµ РїРѕРїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРёРµ
        </h2>

        <div className="grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2">
          {products.map((product) => {
            const isSelected = selected === product.name;
            return (
              <button
                key={product.name}
                onClick={() => setSelected(product.name)}
                className={`group relative overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border p-4 text-left transition-all duration-200 sm:p-5 ${
                  isSelected
                    ? "border-violet-500 bg-violet-500/10 ring-2 ring-violet-500/30"
                    : "border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 hover:border-violet-500/50 hover:bg-zinc-900/80"
                }`}
              >
                <h3 className="text-base font-bold sm:text-lg">
                  {product.name}
                </h3>
                <p className="mt-1 font-bold text-violet-400">
                  {product.priceDisplay}
                </p>

                {isSelected && (
                  <span className="absolute right-3 top-3 flex h-5 w-5 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-violet-500 text-xs">
                    вњ“
                  </span>
                )}
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {selected && (
          <Link
            href={(() => {
              const product = products.find((p) => p.name === selected)!;
              return `/checkout?game=${encodeURIComponent(
                gameName
              )}&product=${encodeURIComponent(
                product.name
              )}&price=${encodeURIComponent(
                product.priceDisplay
              )}&priceUsd=${product.price}&playerInfo=${encodeURIComponent(
                buildPlayerInfo()
              )}`;
            })()}
            className="animate-fade-in-up mt-6 flex w-full items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-2xl bg-gradient-to-r from-violet-600 to-violet-500 py-4 text-center text-lg font-bold shadow-lg shadow-violet-900/30 transition-all duration-200 hover:shadow-xl hover:shadow-violet-900/50 active:scale-[0.98]"
          >
            РљСѓРїРёС‚СЊ Р·Р° {products.find((p) => p.name === selected)?.priceDisplay}
            <span>в†’</span>
          </Link>
        )}
      </div>
    </>
  );
}


===== F:\legendarytopup\app\components\ReviewsSection.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import Link from "next/link";
import { supabase } from "../lib/supabaseClient";
import { useAuth } from "../context/AuthContext";

type Review = {
  id: string;
  user_email: string;
  rating: number;
  text: string;
  created_at: string;
};

function Stars({
  value,
  onChange,
}: {
  value: number;
  onChange?: (n: number) => void;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="flex gap-1">
      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((n) => (
        <button
          key={n}
          type="button"
          disabled={!onChange}
          onClick={() => onChange?.(n)}
          className={`text-2xl leading-none ${
            n <= value ? "text-yellow-400" : "text-zinc-700"
          } ${onChange ? "cursor-pointer" : ""}`}
        >
          в…
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function formatDate(iso: string) {
  return new Date(iso).toLocaleDateString("ru-RU", {
    day: "numeric",
    month: "long",
    year: "numeric",
  });
}

export default function ReviewsSection() {
  const { user, loading: authLoading } = useAuth();

  const [reviews, setReviews] = useState<Review[]>([]);
  const [loadingReviews, setLoadingReviews] = useState(true);

  const [rating, setRating] = useState(0);
  const [text, setText] = useState("");
  const [submitting, setSubmitting] = useState(false);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [visibleCount, setVisibleCount] = useState(6);
  const [hasPurchased, setHasPurchased] = useState(false);
  const [checkingPurchase, setCheckingPurchase] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) {
      setCheckingPurchase(false);
      return;
    }

    async function checkPurchase() {
      const { data } = await supabase
        .from("orders")
        .select("id")
        .eq("user_id", user!.id)
        .limit(1);

      setHasPurchased(Boolean(data && data.length > 0));
      setCheckingPurchase(false);
    }

    checkPurchase();
  }, [user]);

  async function loadReviews() {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from("reviews")
      .select("*")
      .order("created_at", { ascending: false });

    if (data) setReviews(data as Review[]);
    setLoadingReviews(false);
  }

  useEffect(() => {
    loadReviews();
  }, []);

  async function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent) {
    e.preventDefault();
    setError(null);

    if (rating === 0) {
      setError("РџРѕСЃС‚Р°РІСЊС‚Рµ РѕС†РµРЅРєСѓ РѕС‚ 1 РґРѕ 5 Р·РІС‘Р·Рґ");
      return;
    }
    if (!text.trim()) {
      setError("РќР°РїРёС€РёС‚Рµ С‚РµРєСЃС‚ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІР°");
      return;
    }
    if (!user) return;

    setSubmitting(true);

    const { error: insertError } = await supabase.from("reviews").insert({
      user_id: user.id,
      user_email: user.email,
      rating,
      text: text.trim(),
    });

    setSubmitting(false);

    if (insertError) {
      setError("РќРµ РїРѕР»СѓС‡РёР»РѕСЃСЊ РѕС‚РїСЂР°РІРёС‚СЊ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІ. РџРѕРїСЂРѕР±СѓР№С‚Рµ РµС‰С‘ СЂР°Р·.");
      return;
    }

    setRating(0);
    setText("");
    loadReviews();
  }

  return (
    <section id="reviews" className="mx-auto max-w-5xl px-4 py-16 sm:px-6">
      <h2 className="mb-8 text-2xl font-bold sm:text-3xl">РћС‚Р·С‹РІС‹</h2>

      {/* Р¤РѕСЂРјР° РґРѕР±Р°РІР»РµРЅРёСЏ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІР° */}
      <div className="mb-10 rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-5 sm:p-6">
        {authLoading || checkingPurchase ? null : user && hasPurchased ? (
          <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="space-y-4">
            <div>
              <label className="mb-2 block text-sm font-semibold">
                Р’Р°С€Р° РѕС†РµРЅРєР°
              </label>
              <Stars value={rating} onChange={setRating} />
            </div>

            <div>
              <label className="mb-2 block text-sm font-semibold">
                РћС‚Р·С‹РІ
              </label>
              <textarea
                value={text}
                onChange={(e) => setText(e.target.value)}
                rows={3}
                placeholder="Р Р°СЃСЃРєР°Р¶РёС‚Рµ Рѕ СЃРІРѕС‘Рј РѕРїС‹С‚Рµ..."
                className="w-full rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-950 p-3 outline-none focus:border-violet-500"
              />
            </div>

            {error && (
              <p className="rounded-lg bg-red-950/50 p-3 text-sm text-red-400">
                {error}
              </p>
            )}

            <button
              type="submit"
              disabled={submitting}
              className="rounded-xl bg-violet-600 px-6 py-3 font-bold transition hover:bg-violet-500 disabled:opacity-50"
            >
              {submitting ? "РћС‚РїСЂР°РІРєР°..." : "РћСЃС‚Р°РІРёС‚СЊ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІ"}
            </button>
          </form>
        ) : user ? (
          <p className="text-center text-zinc-400">
            РћСЃС‚Р°РІР»СЏС‚СЊ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІС‹ РјРѕРіСѓС‚ С‚РѕР»СЊРєРѕ РїРѕРєСѓРїР°С‚РµР»Рё. РЎРґРµР»Р°Р№С‚Рµ РїРµСЂРІС‹Р№ Р·Р°РєР°Р·,
            С‡С‚РѕР±С‹ РїРѕРґРµР»РёС‚СЊСЃСЏ РІРїРµС‡Р°С‚Р»РµРЅРёРµРј!
          </p>
        ) : (
          <p className="text-center text-zinc-400">
            <Link href="/login" className="text-violet-400 hover:underline">
              Р’РѕР№РґРёС‚Рµ РІ Р°РєРєР°СѓРЅС‚
            </Link>
            , С‡С‚РѕР±С‹ РѕСЃС‚Р°РІРёС‚СЊ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІ
          </p>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* РЎРїРёСЃРѕРє РѕС‚Р·С‹РІРѕРІ */}
      {loadingReviews ? (
        <p className="text-zinc-500">Р—Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєР° РѕС‚Р·С‹РІРѕРІ...</p>
      ) : reviews.length === 0 ? (
        <p className="text-zinc-500">РџРѕРєР° РЅРµС‚ РѕС‚Р·С‹РІРѕРІ вЂ” Р±СѓРґСЊС‚Рµ РїРµСЂРІС‹Рј!</p>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4 sm:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3">
            {reviews.slice(0, visibleCount).map((review) => (
              <div
                key={review.id}
                className="rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-5 transition hover:border-violet-500/50"
              >
                <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
                  <div className="flex h-10 w-10 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-violet-600 font-bold uppercase">
                    {review.user_email[0]}
                  </div>

                  <div className="flex-1">
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-x-3 gap-y-1">
                      <span className="font-semibold text-white">
                        {review.user_email.split("@")[0]}
                      </span>
                      <span className="text-xs text-zinc-500">
                        {formatDate(review.created_at)}
                      </span>
                    </div>

                    <div className="mt-1">
                      <Stars value={review.rating} />
                    </div>

                    <p className="mt-3 text-zinc-300">{review.text}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          {visibleCount < reviews.length && (
            <div className="mt-8 text-center">
              <button
                onClick={() => setVisibleCount((prev) => prev + 6)}
                className="rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 px-6 py-3 font-semibold transition hover:border-violet-500 hover:bg-zinc-900"
              >
                РџРѕРєР°Р·Р°С‚СЊ РµС‰С‘
              </button>
            </div>
          )}
        </>
      )}
    </section>
  );
}

"use client";

import { useEffect, useState, useRef } from "react";
import { createClient } from "../lib/supabase/client";

type Message = {
  id: string;
  session_id: string;
  sender: string;
  message: string;
  created_at: string;
};

function getSessionId() {
  if (typeof window === "undefined") return "";
  let id = localStorage.getItem("support_session_id");
  if (!id) {
    id = crypto.randomUUID();
    localStorage.setItem("support_session_id", id);
  }
  return id;
}

function newSessionId() {
  const id = crypto.randomUUID();
  localStorage.setItem("support_session_id", id);
  return id;
}

function formatTime(iso: string) {
  const date = new Date(iso);
  return date.toLocaleTimeString("ru-RU", {
    hour: "2-digit",
    minute: "2-digit",
  });
}

const ORIGINAL_TITLE = typeof document !== "undefined" ? document.title : "";

export default function SupportWidget() {
  const supabase = createClient();
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState("");
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<Message[]>([]);
  const [text, setText] = useState("");
  const [unread, setUnread] = useState(0);
  const [adminOnline, setAdminOnline] = useState(false);
  const [adminTyping, setAdminTyping] = useState(false);
  const [confirmReset, setConfirmReset] = useState(false);

  const bottomRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const roomChannelRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof supabase.channel> | null>(null);
  const typingTimeoutRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
  const titleIntervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval> | null>(null);
  const openRef = useRef(open);

  useEffect(() => {
    openRef.current = open;
  }, [open]);

  useEffect(() => {
    setSessionId(getSessionId());
  }, []);

  // РћРЅР»Р°Р№РЅ-СЃС‚Р°С‚СѓСЃ Р°РґРјРёРЅР°
  useEffect(() => {
    const presenceChannel = supabase.channel("admin_presence");
    presenceChannel
      .on("presence", { event: "sync" }, () => {
        const state = presenceChannel.presenceState();
        setAdminOnline(Object.keys(state).length > 0);
      })
      .subscribe();

    return () => {
      supabase.removeChannel(presenceChannel);
    };
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!sessionId) return;

    async function loadMessages() {
      const { data } = await supabase
        .from("support_messages")
        .select("*")
        .eq("session_id", sessionId)
        .order("created_at", { ascending: true });
      if (data) setMessages(data as Message[]);
    }

    loadMessages();

    const channel = supabase
      .channel("support_room", {
        config: { broadcast: { self: false } },
      })
      .on("broadcast", { event: "message" }, ({ payload }) => {
        const incoming = payload as Message;
        if (incoming.session_id !== sessionId) return;

        setMessages((prev) =>
          prev.some((m) => m.id === incoming.id) ? prev : [...prev, incoming]
        );

        if (incoming.sender === "admin") {
          setAdminTyping(false);
          if (!openRef.current || document.hidden) {
            setUnread((prev) => prev + 1);
            try {
              new Audio(
                "data:audio/wav;base64,UklGRhwAAABXQVZFZm10IBAAAAABAAEAQB8AAEAfAAABAAgAZGF0YQAAAAA="
              ).play();
            } catch {}
          }
        }
      })
      .on("broadcast", { event: "typing" }, ({ payload }) => {
        if (payload.session_id !== sessionId) return;
        if (payload.sender !== "admin") return;
        setAdminTyping(true);
        if (typingTimeoutRef.current) clearTimeout(typingTimeoutRef.current);
        typingTimeoutRef.current = setTimeout(() => setAdminTyping(false), 2500);
      })
      .subscribe();

    roomChannelRef.current = channel;

    return () => {
      supabase.removeChannel(channel);
    };
  }, [sessionId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (unread > 0 && document.hidden) {
      let showAlert = true;
      titleIntervalRef.current = setInterval(() => {
        document.title = showAlert ? "рџ’¬ РќРѕРІРѕРµ СЃРѕРѕР±С‰РµРЅРёРµ!" : ORIGINAL_TITLE;
        showAlert = !showAlert;
      }, 1200);
    } else {
      if (titleIntervalRef.current) clearInterval(titleIntervalRef.current);
      document.title = ORIGINAL_TITLE;
    }
    return () => {
      if (titleIntervalRef.current) clearInterval(titleIntervalRef.current);
    };
  }, [unread]);

  useEffect(() => {
    function handleVisibility() {
      if (!document.hidden && open) setUnread(0);
    }
    document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", handleVisibility);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("visibilitychange", handleVisibility);
  }, [open]);

  useEffect(() => {
    bottomRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
  }, [messages, open, adminTyping]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (open) setUnread(0);
  }, [open]);

  function handleTextChange(value: string) {
    setText(value);
    roomChannelRef.current?.send({
      type: "broadcast",
      event: "typing",
      payload: { sender: "user", session_id: sessionId },
    });
  }

  async function handleSend() {
    const trimmed = text.trim();
    if (!trimmed) return;

    const tempId = `temp-${Date.now()}`;
    const optimisticMessage: Message = {
      id: tempId,
      session_id: sessionId,
      sender: "user",
      message: trimmed,
      created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    setMessages((prev) => [...prev, optimisticMessage]);
    setText("");

    const { data, error } = await supabase
      .from("support_messages")
      .insert({ session_id: sessionId, sender: "user", message: trimmed })
      .select()
      .single();

    if (error) {
      setMessages((prev) => prev.filter((m) => m.id !== tempId));
      return;
    }

    const saved = data as Message;
    setMessages((prev) => prev.map((m) => (m.id === tempId ? saved : m)));

    roomChannelRef.current?.send({
      type: "broadcast",
      event: "message",
      payload: saved,
    });

    // Р•СЃР»Рё РґРёР°Р»РѕРі Р±С‹Р» Р·Р°РєСЂС‹С‚ Р°РґРјРёРЅРѕРј вЂ” РїРµСЂРµРѕС‚РєСЂС‹РІР°РµРј РµРіРѕ
    await supabase
      .from("support_sessions")
      .upsert({ session_id: sessionId, status: "open", updated_at: new Date().toISOString() });

    roomChannelRef.current?.send({
      type: "broadcast",
      event: "session_status",
      payload: { session_id: sessionId, status: "open" },
    });
  }

  function handleStartNewChat() {
    const id = newSessionId();
    setMessages([]);
    setSessionId(id);
    setConfirmReset(false);
  }

  return (
    <div className="fixed bottom-4 right-4 z-50 sm:bottom-6 sm:right-6">
      {open && (
        <div className="animate-fade-in-up mb-4 flex h-[70vh] max-h-96 w-[90vw] max-w-80 flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900/95 shadow-2xl backdrop-blur">
          <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-gradient-to-r from-violet-600 to-violet-500 px-4 py-3">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
              <span
                className={`h-2 w-2 rounded-full transition-colors duration-300 ${
                  adminOnline ? "animate-pulse bg-emerald-400" : "bg-zinc-400"
                }`}
              />
              <div>
                <p className="font-bold text-white leading-tight">РџРѕРґРґРµСЂР¶РєР°</p>
                <p className="text-[11px] text-white/70 leading-tight transition-opacity duration-200">
                  {adminOnline ? "РћРЅР»Р°Р№РЅ вЂ” РѕС‚РІРµС‡Р°РµРј СЃРµР№С‡Р°СЃ" : "РћР±С‹С‡РЅРѕ РѕС‚РІРµС‡Р°РµРј Р±С‹СЃС‚СЂРѕ"}
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <button
                onClick={() => setConfirmReset(true)}
                title="РќР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ РЅРѕРІС‹Р№ РґРёР°Р»РѕРі"
                className="text-white/70 transition-colors duration-150 hover:text-white"
              >
                рџ”„
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setOpen(false)}
                className="text-white/80 transition-colors duration-150 hover:text-white"
              >
                вњ•
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>

          {confirmReset && (
            <div className="animate-fade-in flex items-center justify-between gap-2 border-b border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 px-4 py-2 text-xs">
              <span className="text-zinc-400">РћС‡РёСЃС‚РёС‚СЊ РёСЃС‚РѕСЂРёСЋ Рё РЅР°С‡Р°С‚СЊ Р·Р°РЅРѕРІРѕ?</span>
              <div className="flex gap-2">
                <button
                  onClick={handleStartNewChat}
                  className="font-semibold text-violet-400 hover:text-violet-300"
                >
                  Р”Р°
                </button>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setConfirmReset(false)}
                  className="text-zinc-500 hover:text-zinc-300"
                >
                  РћС‚РјРµРЅР°
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="flex-1 space-y-3 overflow-y-auto p-4">
            {messages.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-sm text-zinc-500">
                Р”РѕР±СЂРѕ РїРѕР¶Р°Р»РѕРІР°С‚СЊ! РќР°РїРёС€РёС‚Рµ РЅР°Рј, С‡РµРј РјРѕР¶РµРј РїРѕРјРѕС‡СЊ.
              </p>
            )}

            {messages.map((m) => (
              <div
                key={m.id}
                className={`animate-fade-in flex flex-col ${
                  m.sender === "admin" ? "items-start" : "items-end"
                }`}
              >
                <div
                  className={`max-w-[80%] rounded-2xl px-3 py-2 text-sm ${
                    m.sender === "admin"
                      ? "bg-zinc-800 text-white"
                      : "bg-gradient-to-r from-violet-600 to-violet-500 text-white"
                  }`}
                >
                  {m.message}
                </div>
                <span className="mt-1 px-1 text-[10px] text-zinc-500">
                  {formatTime(m.created_at)}

            ))}

            {adminTyping && (
              <div className="animate-fade-in flex items-center gap-1 px-1">

                <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-bounce rounded-full bg-zinc-500 [animation-delay:-0.15s]" />
                <span className="h-1.5 w-1.5 animate-bounce rounded-full bg-zinc-500" />

===== F:\legendarytopup\app\context\AuthContext.tsx =====

"use client";

import { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from "react";
import type { User } from "@supabase/supabase-js";
import { supabase } from "../lib/supabaseClient";

type AuthContextType = {
  user: User | null;
  loading: boolean;
  signOut: () => Promise<void>;
};

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType>({
  user: null,
  loading: true,
  signOut: async () => {},
});

export function AuthProvider({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  const [user, setUser] = useState<User | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    // РџСЂРѕРІРµСЂСЏРµРј, Р·Р°Р»РѕРіРёРЅРµРЅ Р»Рё РїРѕР»СЊР·РѕРІР°С‚РµР»СЊ РїСЂРё Р·Р°РіСЂСѓР·РєРµ СЃС‚СЂР°РЅРёС†С‹
    supabase.auth.getSession().then(({ data }) => {
      setUser(data.session?.user ?? null);
      setLoading(false);
    });

    // РџРѕРґРїРёСЃС‹РІР°РµРјСЃСЏ РЅР° РёР·РјРµРЅРµРЅРёСЏ (РІС…РѕРґ/РІС‹С…РѕРґ)
    const { data: listener } = supabase.auth.onAuthStateChange(
      (_event, session) => {
        setUser(session?.user ?? null);
      }
    );

    return () => {
      listener.subscription.unsubscribe();
    };
  }, []);

  async function signOut() {
    await supabase.auth.signOut();
  }

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, loading, signOut }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

export function useAuth() {
  return useContext(AuthContext);
}


===== F:\legendarytopup\app\data\games.ts =====

// ============================================================
// РљРѕРЅС„РёРіСѓСЂР°С†РёСЏ С†РµРЅ
// ============================================================
// РљСѓСЂСЃ РѕР±РјРµРЅР° USD -> UZS (РѕР±РЅРѕРІРё РїСЂРё РёР·РјРµРЅРµРЅРёРё РєСѓСЂСЃР°)
export const EXCHANGE_RATE_UZS_PER_USD = 12100;

// РќР°С†РµРЅРєР° СЃРІРµСЂС… Р±Р°Р·РѕРІРѕР№ СЃРµР±РµСЃС‚РѕРёРјРѕСЃС‚Рё (0.15 = +15%)
export const MARKUP = 0.15;

// РџРµСЂРµРІРѕРґРёС‚ С†РµРЅСѓ РІ СЃСѓРјР°С… (СЃРµР±РµСЃС‚РѕРёРјРѕСЃС‚СЊ) РІ С„РёРЅР°Р»СЊРЅСѓСЋ С†РµРЅСѓ РІ USD СЃ РЅР°С†РµРЅРєРѕР№
function toUsd(priceInSum) {
  const base = priceInSum / EXCHANGE_RATE_UZS_PER_USD;
  const withMarkup = base * (1 + MARKUP);
  return Math.round(withMarkup * 100) / 100; // РѕРєСЂСѓРіР»РµРЅРёРµ РґРѕ С†РµРЅС‚РѕРІ
}

// Р¤РѕСЂРјР°С‚РёСЂСѓРµС‚ С‡РёСЃР»Рѕ РІ РѕС‚РѕР±СЂР°Р¶Р°РµРјСѓСЋ СЃС‚СЂРѕРєСѓ С†РµРЅС‹, РЅР°РїСЂ. 9.03 -> "$9.03"
export function formatPrice(amountUsd) {
  return `$${amountUsd.toFixed(2)}`;
}

// РЎРѕР±РёСЂР°РµС‚ РіРѕС‚РѕРІС‹Р№ РѕР±СЉРµРєС‚ С‚РѕРІР°СЂР°: Рё С‡РёСЃР»Рѕ (РґР»СЏ СЂР°СЃС‡С‘С‚РѕРІ),
// Рё СЃС‚СЂРѕРєСѓ СЃРѕ Р·РЅР°РєРѕРј $ (РґР»СЏ РѕС‚РѕР±СЂР°Р¶РµРЅРёСЏ РІ UI)
function product(name, priceInSum) {
  const price = toUsd(priceInSum);
  return { name, price, priceDisplay: formatPrice(price) };
}

// ============================================================
// Р”Р°РЅРЅС‹Рµ РёРіСЂ
// ============================================================
export const games = [
  {
    name: "PUBG Mobile",
    slug: "pubg-mobile",
    image: "/games/pubg.jpg",
    fields: [{ label: "PUBG ID", placeholder: "Р’РІРµРґРёС‚Рµ PUBG ID" }],
    products: [
      product("60 UC", 18000),
      product("325 UC", 95000),
      product("660 UC", 160000),
      product("1800 UC", 370000),
    ],
  },

  {
    name: "Brawl Stars",
    slug: "brawl-stars",
    image: "/games/br.jpg",
    fields: [{ label: "Player Tag", placeholder: "Р’РІРµРґРёС‚Рµ #С‚РµРі РёРіСЂРѕРєР°" }],
    products: [

===== F:\legendarytopup\app\games\[slug]\page.tsx =====

"use client";

import { useState } from "react";
import { games } from "../../data/games";
import { notFound } from "next/navigation";
import Link from "next/link";
import { useParams } from "next/navigation";

export default function GamePage() {
  const params = useParams();
  const slug = params.slug as string;

  const game = games.find((g) => g.slug === slug);

  const [fieldValues, setFieldValues] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});

  if (!game) {
    notFound();
  }

  function handleFieldChange(label: string, value: string) {
    setFieldValues((prev) => ({ ...prev, [label]: value }));
  }

  function buildPlayerInfo() {
    return JSON.stringify(fieldValues);
  }

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-zinc-950 text-white">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-10 sm:px-6 sm:py-16">
        <div className="grid gap-8 lg:grid-cols-2 lg:gap-12">
          <div>
            <img
              src={game.image}
              alt={game.name}
              className="w-full rounded-3xl border border-zinc-800 shadow-2xl"
            />
          </div>

          <div>
            <span className="rounded-full bg-violet-600 px-4 py-2 text-xs font-bold sm:text-sm">
              вљЎ РњРѕРјРµРЅС‚Р°Р»СЊРЅРѕРµ РїРѕРїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРёРµ
            </span>

            <h1 className="mt-6 text-3xl font-bold sm:text-4xl md:text-5xl">
              {game.name}
            </h1>

            <p className="mt-4 text-base text-zinc-400 sm:text-lg">
              РџРѕРїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРёРµ {game.name} Р±С‹СЃС‚СЂРѕ Рё Р±РµР·РѕРїР°СЃРЅРѕ.
            </p>

            <div className="mt-8 space-y-5 sm:mt-10">
              {game.fields.map((field) => (
                <div key={field.label}>
                  <label className="mb-2 block font-semibold">
                    {field.label}
                  </label>

                  <input
                    placeholder={field.placeholder}
                    value={fieldValues[field.label] ?? ""}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      handleFieldChange(field.label, e.target.value)
                    }
                    className="w-full rounded-xl border border-zinc-700 bg-zinc-900 p-4 outline-none transition-colors duration-200 focus:border-violet-500"
                  />
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            <div className="mt-8 sm:mt-10">
              <h2 className="mb-5 text-xl font-bold sm:text-2xl">
                Р’С‹Р±РµСЂРёС‚Рµ РїРѕРїРѕР»РЅРµРЅРёРµ
              </h2>

              <div className="space-y-4">
                {game.products.map((product) => (
                  <div
                    key={product.name}
                    className="flex flex-col gap-4 rounded-2xl border border-zinc-800 bg-zinc-900 p-4 transition-all duration-200 hover:border-violet-500 hover:bg-zinc-900/80 sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between sm:p-5"
                  >
                    <div>
                      <h3 className="text-lg font-bold sm:text-xl">
                        {product.name}
                      </h3>

                      <p className="mt-1 font-bold text-violet-400">
                        {product.priceDisplay}
                      </p>
                    </div>

                    <Link
                      href={`/checkout?game=${encodeURIComponent(
                        game.name
                      )}&product=${encodeURIComponent(
                        product.name
                      )}&price=${encodeURIComponent(
                        product.priceDisplay
                      )}&priceUsd=${product.price}&playerInfo=${encodeURIComponent(
                        buildPlayerInfo()
                      )}`}
                      className="w-full rounded-xl bg-violet-600 px-6 py-3 text-center font-bold transition-colors duration-200 hover:bg-violet-500 active:scale-[0.98] sm:w-auto"
                    >
                      РљСѓРїРёС‚СЊ
                    </Link>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}


===== F:\legendarytopup\app\lib\supabase\client.ts =====

import { createBrowserClient } from "@supabase/ssr";

export function createClient() {
  return createBrowserClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!
  );
}


===== F:\legendarytopup\app\lib\supabase\server.ts =====

import { createServerClient } from "@supabase/ssr";
import { cookies } from "next/headers";

export async function createClient() {
  const cookieStore = await cookies();

  return createServerClient(
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!,
    process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!,
    {
      cookies: {
        getAll() {
          return cookieStore.getAll();
        },
        setAll(cookiesToSet) {
          try {
            cookiesToSet.forEach(({ name, value, options }) =>
              cookieStore.set(name, value, options)
            );
          } catch {}
        },
      },
    }
  );
}


===== F:\legendarytopup\app\lib\adminPin.ts =====

import crypto from "crypto";

export const COOKIE_NAME = "admin_pin_ok";
const TTL_MS = 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 12 С‡Р°СЃРѕРІ

function sign(payload: string) {
  const secret = process.env.ADMIN_PIN_SECRET!;
  return crypto.createHmac("sha256", secret).update(payload).digest("hex");
}

export function createPinCookieValue() {
  const expires = Date.now() + TTL_MS;
  const payload = `${expires}`;
  const sig = sign(payload);
  return `${payload}.${sig}`;
}

export function isPinCookieValid(value: string | undefined) {
  if (!value) return false;
  const [payload, sig] = value.split(".");
  if (!payload || !sig) return false;
  if (sign(payload) !== sig) return false;
  const expires = Number(payload);
  if (Number.isNaN(expires) || Date.now() > expires) return false;
  return true;
}
